◎ Zhangzhou Pacification Conference 81

Fang Shengtao Has Returned to the Province from Southern Fujian

Fuzhou Correspondence: Cai Tingkai, Commander-in-Chief of the 19th Route Army and Acting Pacification Commissioner stationed in Fujian, convened a pacification conference at the Zhangzhou Pacification Commissioner's Office on the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd of this month, gathering military and political officials from the four districts of Western Fujian, Southern Fujian, Tinglong, Zhangzhou, and Quanzhou to discuss specific measures for bandit suppression, village cleansing, road construction, financial management, and rent reduction. The following is an excerpt: (A) Regarding Bandit Suppression: (1) Before the main force of the Red Bandits is defeated, pacification will be carried out in separate zones. (2) The county magistrate, in cooperation with the stationed troops, will have three months to suppress and clear out the remaining bandits in each county. Those who conceal and do not report will be punished as accomplices of bandits. (3) Those who can genuinely repent and surrender, regardless of whether they are Red Bandits or local bandits, will be allowed to surrender their weapons. However, it is strictly forbidden to incorporate bandits into the army. (B) Regarding Village Cleansing: (1) At the beginning of the recovery of bandit areas, village cleansing should be carried out immediately. Local administrative and party affairs will be handled by the local military commander first. (2) The Lianjia system should be established according to the regulations issued by the central government to investigate household registration and implement joint defense. (3) Guide the villages and towns to raise funds to selectively build blockhouses and earthen forts. (C) Regarding the Organization of Local Militias: (1) The local militias in each county will be under the jurisdiction of the county magistrate and under the command of the military commander. (2) Militia members will be divided into active and reserve categories. It is not allowed to recruit foreigners. (3) Strictly prevent local bullies from manipulating the local militias to oppress the people. (D) Regarding Road Construction: (1) The main road connecting Western Fujian to Southern Fujian will be handled by the Construction Department under the order of the Provincial Government from the Pacification Office. The branch roads in each county will be actively repaired by the county magistrate separately. (2) The road construction fee will be 300,000 yuan from the rice tax of Xicheng (i.e., Longxi and Haicheng counties), 300,000 yuan from the salt tax surcharge of Zhangzhou, and 300,000 yuan borrowed from highway vehicle rental, totaling 900,000 yuan. Once this amount is collected, the various taxes will be cancelled. (E) Regarding Financial Management: (1) Issue a general order requiring all military and political agencies to publish the exact amount of revenue and expenditure on a monthly basis. (2) The Pacification Office will send a letter to the Provincial Government ordering the financial commissioner to sort out and eliminate various exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies separately, and the Pacification Office will order the various troops to supervise the implementation. (F) Regarding Rent Reduction: (1) Submit a request to the central government to issue a new solution to the land problem in the bandit suppression area. (2) Before the central government's solution is issued, a temporary rent reduction of 25% will be implemented.

Fang Shengtao, Acting Chairman of the Provincial Government, and Commissioner Lin Zhiyuan recently went to Xinghua and Yongchun to inspect the two brigades of the Provincial Defense Army, Chen Guohui and Chen Wei Yuan, and arranged to meet with Cai Tingkai to discuss the defense area of the Provincial Defense Army in Southern Fujian. It has been found that after Fang arrived in Quanzhou, he met with Division Commander Mao Weishou and then returned to the province on the 9th with Chen Guohui on two planes. Therefore, he has not yet been able to meet with Cai. However, it is heard that the General Headquarters of the 19th Route Army has decided to transfer three regiments of the First Supplementary Brigade, led by Tan Qixiu, to Fuzhou within a few days for the Pacification Office to dispatch. The former Army School in front of the Junmen in the city has been designated as the brigade headquarters. (August 10)

◎ The Tiger Plague is Rampant in Shandong Province 82

Deaths Continue in the Plague Area

No One Carries and Buries the Corpses

Jinan Correspondence: Recently, the tiger plague has spread in various parts of northern and western Shandong Province, causing many deaths. The worst case is in Lijin City, where shops in the city streets dare not open for business, and most residents also close their doors and stay indoors. Looking at the streets, there is no trace of people. There are two hospitals in the city, but their directors have also died, causing their partners to disperse and close down one after another. Coffins are sold out, and the dead have no way to be encoffined. The county government informs that those who die of the plague must be carried out and buried within a few hours. No one is willing to serve as the funeral procession, the mourning musicians, or the pallbearers. It costs ten yuan for each corpse carried from the city to the suburbs for burial. Those who engage in this business do so at the risk of their lives, often burying people before burying others. Next is Zhanhua. Since the beginning of August, the tiger plague has occurred, causing many deaths in various places. Soldiers of the 59th Brigade of the stationed army have also died from this plague. It is heard that two soldiers have died in the brigade headquarters. The situation in the 117th Regiment is even more severe. After abdominal pain, they immediately faint and can die in just two hours. In order to prevent the spread of the tiger plague, Zhou Xiaoyi, Deputy Brigade Commander of the 59th Brigade, has ordered the officers of each department to gather the soldiers under their command to explain the methods of epidemic prevention and to telegraph the division headquarters to issue a large number of epidemic prevention drugs. County Magistrate Zhuang Shouchong is working hard to guide the people in epidemic prevention to prevent the spread. Huxian, Beixiang, and Huji areas have also discovered the tiger plague. Patients vomit, have diarrhea, or convulsions. The symptoms are dangerous and there is no cure. In the Huji area, hundreds of people have died in the past five or six days. The urban area has also discovered this plague, with six or seven deaths. In order to prevent the spread of the epidemic, the county government has convened epidemic prevention meetings for several days and organized an epidemic prevention committee, which will go to various villages to provide relief. Yidu has also recently discovered the tiger plague, especially in the urban area. According to a reliable investigation by the county Public Security Bureau, there have been more than 170 deaths from the tiger plague in the city. Also, people from Changqing reported that cholera (i.e., cholera) has been discovered in the southeastern township of the county, causing many deaths. The situation in Niujiaogou Village is even more severe, with the number of deaths accounting for one-half of the entire village. Even one person who is infected will infect the whole family, and the whole family will die. In order to avoid infection, no one carries and buries the corpses. Patients are numerous in dozens of nearby villages. Chinese medicine practitioners in the countryside are helpless. People are uneasy, agricultural work is abandoned, and the fields are barren. The autumn harvest is reduced, and the people's livelihood is extremely difficult. (August 14)

◎ Northeast Postal Workers Arrive in Jinan

Talking About the Hardships of Escaping Danger and Entering the Customs

Jinan Correspondence: Since our country implemented the blockade of the postal service in the Northeast, the tyrannical Japan has instigated the puppet state to privately set up a post office. However, all the old postal workers, with a strong sense of patriotism, were unwilling to be driven by the enemy and planned to enter the customs as a whole to seek another livelihood. However, the Japanese learned of this in advance and dispatched puppet police to patrol the post office and the vicinity of the staff dormitory day and night. Anyone who wanted to move out was arrested and subjected to extreme torture. The patriotic postal workers had to disguise themselves as merchants and farmers and mix into the customs. In recent days, more than 1,500 people have gathered in Tianjin. There are also those who were arrested halfway and their whereabouts are unknown. All the postal workers who have entered the customs have been assigned to work in the post offices in Beiping, Tianjin, Qingdao, and Shanghai. More than a dozen postal clerks have arrived in Jinan and have been properly settled and started working. The Jinan Post Office has specially organized a temporary reception center for Northeast postal workers to receive postal workers who continue to come to Shandong. People have been sent to the station every day to welcome and receive them. At 7:30 this morning, 97 postal workers arrived in Jinan on the 9th train from Tianjin-Pukou. After getting off the train, they were led by the reception staff to the post office to rest and eat. According to the representatives Qin Yunzhang, Yang Yushan, Huang Dengge, and Chen Zhongxiu, a total of 100 postal workers came to Jinan this time. Three people were left in Tianjin due to illness. The 97 people who actually arrived in Jinan were all workers and clerks who had been serving in Yingkou, Jinzhou, Liaoning, and Andong. The puppet government organized by Japan originally planned to take over the post office on August 1, but we received an order from the national government on July 20 to stop work. The Japanese heard the news and immediately sent military police to the bureau to force us to resume work and promote and increase salaries to buy people's hearts. We all refused to be intimidated and lured and disguised ourselves as ordinary people and merchants to escape into the customs. If we were careless on the way, we would be arrested and subjected to extreme torture. Some were even shot by them. We entered the customs by land and sea. Those who traveled by land took the Beining train and were severely inspected and questioned by the puppet police along the way. A slight oversight would lead to falling into the tiger's mouth. Once, someone held a "Daoxiangcun" card to prove that he was a merchant of that company. The difficulties along the way can be imagined. Those who traveled by sea went to Tianjin from Yingkou or to Shanghai from Dalian. The Japanese forced the postal workers in Yingkou to sign a condition that the Japanese would recruit new workers and the old employees would act as instructors to teach all the work procedures to the new workers before they could leave. Fortunately, our government had already blockaded the postal service in the Northeast at that time, and the number of letters received every day was small, so there was not much work. Therefore, the new workers could easily learn to do it. After a few days, they said that they were familiar with the procedures, so we took the opportunity to leave the place. However, the inspection was extremely strict when boarding the ship from Yingkou. We still did not dare to call our colleagues postal workers. We don't know why several colleagues were arrested by them. We didn't dare to rescue them either. We don't know where they are now. No matter how many colleagues there were on the ship or train, no one dared to talk to each other, pretending not to know each other. Even if we saw our colleagues being forced away, we didn't dare to speak up. It is the so-called daring to be angry but not daring to speak. Now we are lucky to have escaped from the tiger's mouth and returned to our country, but there are still thousands of colleagues and 30 million compatriots in the Northeast who are being killed and ravaged by the tyrannical Japan every day. We hope that the people of the country will rise up and rescue them. The work location of our arrival in Jinan has not yet been designated, so we can only wait for the assignment. All our families have been abandoned outside the customs, and their survival is unpredictable. It is also heard that when the postal workers arrived in Tianjin, each person received five yuan from the donations of various groups. There was not much left after arriving in Jinan, and the post office work was urgent and could not be obtained, so we had to sit and eat nothing. We urgently need the relief of all sectors of society. (August 14)

◎ The Lingbi People's Uprising Expands 83

Tong County Sends Troops to Defend Against Rioters Crossing the Border

Xuzhou Correspondence: Residents of Youji, Fifth District, Lingbi County, northern Anhui, recently planned to demand that the county government return the tobacco tax they had paid. They gathered a crowd to riot, destroyed the entire district office, beat public officials to death, and kidnapped township chiefs. Jiang Dingwen, commander of the Second Army stationed in Bengbu, summoned the Lingbi County Magistrate to Bengbu after receiving a telegram to inquire about the truth and sent personnel to the scene of the incident to investigate in detail. Unexpectedly, the people's uprising expanded more and more and was about to invade the Jiangsu border. The Lingbi County Government could not resolve the situation, so it invited impartial people with some reputation in the local area to persuade the people in the district, but to no avail. It is now heard that the rioters have increased to more than 4,000 people and claim that they will eliminate those who have harmed the people in the past. It is estimated that they have occupied Dali Ji, Yang Shan, Wang Ji, Yu Gou, Yang Tong, Jiu Ji, Shili Dian, Zhang Da Lu, Feng Jia Miao, Huitang Gou, You Ji Shang Zhu Jia, Yugou Chaoyang and other places, resulting in the abandonment of agricultural work and no one to care for the autumn harvest. All traffic between Lingbi and Tongshan has also been destroyed by the rioters. The Lingbi County Police Force is afraid that the rioters will seize its firearms and has detoured to the Shuanggou Town on the border of Tong and Lingbi to temporarily avoid them. The Suining County Police Force in the Lingbi and Suining border is also on alert, but they all feel that they are outnumbered and fear that they will be difficult to resist. The Tongshan County Government, according to the request of the Eighth District, specially dispatched a cavalry team led by Guo Yubiao to Shuanggou Town to garrison against unforeseen circumstances. Guo sent someone to the city at noon on the 13th to report that the people's uprising in Lingbi was caused by the oppression of local bullies. The people used the excuse of resisting the tobacco tax to confiscate most of the self-defense firearms in various villages and gathered thousands of people with a powerful momentum. The police force in the county was unable to resist and retreated to Shuanggou Town on the 11th. That night, 13 self-defense guns in the Baoyu within the Shuanggou West Jiu Li were forcibly taken away by Xie Guangming, a resident of the Baoyu. The Yang self-defense guns in the Gaozhuang, Qili, were also looted. It is also heard that the Lingbi County sent local gentry to persuade the people, but to no avail, and the situation became more serious. At present, the rioters are only 20 to 30 miles away from Shuanggou. Once they invade, how should our team deal with it? Therefore, we sent a telegram to ask for instructions. The Tongshan County Government was afraid that the rioters in Lingbi would cross the border and riot, so it telegraphed the Provincial Government and the Security Office on the 12th to ask for instructions on how to deal with the situation. It received a reply on the 13th, which read: (1) Magistrate Yang Jianwen telegram received. I have telegraphed Chairman Wu of Anhui to quickly order a stop. You should still properly prevent it and do not neglect it. Chairman Gu Yuan. (2) Magistrate Yang Jianwen Jianwen telegram received. If the order of Tong border is violated, use force to stop it and report the situation to Li Mingyang at any time. Yuan County Government, according to the telegram reply, immediately sent another company commander, Han Deping, with 60 police soldiers to assist.

◎ Bandit News from the Border of Jiangsu, Anhui, and Henan 84

Wu Qi's Bandit Gang Invades Wuhe

Li Chenggong's Gang Flees to Haoxian

Bengbu Correspondence: The banditry in Anhui Province has not been eradicated after years of suppression. Recently, the banditry situation at the border of Jiangsu, Henan, and Anhui is still extremely rampant. The situation of suppressing bandits is recorded as follows:

Border of Jiangsu and Anhui: The areas of Xuyi and Sixian in northern Anhui are close to Hongze Lake and adjacent to Jiangsu, with crisscrossing waterways, and have always been a breeding ground for bandits. The major bandit Wei Yisan's gang has been rampant between Jiangsu and Anhui for several years. Previously, the 25th Route Army Liang Guanying's troops repeatedly encircled and suppressed the bandits, causing them great damage. Recently, Liang's troops were transferred to Anhui to suppress the communists, and the gang became rampant again between Jiangsu and Anhui. Bandit leader Wu Qi led a crowd of five or six hundred people to run amok in the Xuyi and Wuhe areas. A few days ago, they successively occupied Huaining Town, Fushan Town, Yangtai, Liutai, Zhaotai, Dingba, Daliuheng and other towns and villages in Xuyi, looting more than two hundred rifles from the local militias, and committed all kinds of atrocities such as burning, killing and looting. Recently, they have even invaded Wuhe County. Song Zhinan, the magistrate of Wuhe County, immediately sent the county's reserve team to block them, and they arrived on the south bank of the Huai River. On the morning of the 12th, the county police exchanged fire with the bandits across the river. Knowing that there was preparation, the bandits immediately retreated to Xuyi. The Wuhe County Government has now telegraphed the Anhui Provincial Government requesting that troops be sent to suppress the bandits severely to ensure local security.

Border of Henan and Anhui: The three gangs of notorious bandits Li Chenggong, Liu Laoqi, and Wei Quezi in eastern Henan recently took advantage of the autumn harvest season to gather more than a thousand people and occupy the border area of Shangqiu, Zhecheng, Luyi, and Haoxian. The long-distance telephone lines of each county were cut off, and news was therefore isolated. Many people fled. Zhang Zhankui, the brigade commander of the 14th Cavalry Brigade stationed in Guide, upon receiving the report, led his troops to Qiukou on the 8th, and sent the 3rd Company to suppress the bandits in Liuqiao and Qiukou. The bandits initially resisted stubbornly, but after Zhang's troops bravely charged, more than ten bandits were killed on the spot. The bandits then fled in panic to Songji to the south of the border between Hao and Shang, and the Wanglou and Liqiao areas. Zhang's brigade pursued them. That night, the bandits tried to flee west from Songji. After Zhang's brigade used machine guns to strafe them, the bandits fled to the Songyanji area of Haoxian County in Anhui. In this battle, more than fifty bandits were killed, more than a hundred men and women were rescued, and a great number of spoils of war were seized. (14th)

◎ Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture Design Conference 85

The Sericulture Design Committee convened by the Jiangsu Industrial Department held its first general meeting on the 13th. The second and third general meetings were held on the 14th, in the morning and afternoon respectively. The closing ceremony was held on the same evening. The details are summarized as follows:

Meeting Situation: The following committee members attended the first general meeting: Tan Xihong, He Yushu, Leng Yuqiu, Ge Jingzhong, Lufei Zhi (represented by Guan Yida), Bao Mingshu, He Shangping, Liao Jianan, Sun Benzhong, Shen Yi, Shan Changqi, Xu Zhen, Qian Fenghao, Miao Zhongxiu, Yi Tingjian, Qi Lunjie, Xue Shouxuan, Fei Dasheng, Gu Ying, Zhu Jingan, Xia Zhenduo, Shao Shenpei. Observers included: Hou Zhenping, Jiang Nanchun, Tang Xixiang, Ni Shaoyun, Tang Jianzhong, Jiang Kesheng, Gu Ming, Tai Qirui, Bei Shibang, Zhou Yuangong, Zhang Xian, Zhang Zifang, Zhang Wenming. Chairman He Yushu reported on the purpose of the meeting. Director Tan of the Industrial Department reported on the decline of the Chinese silk industry and the efforts made by various parties to provide relief. Committee Member Qi reported on the situation of the sericulture improvement model area in Jintan County. Committee Member Leng reported on the opinions on reclaiming wasteland, planting mulberry trees, and improving the sericulture industry. After the reports, the chairman proposed the organization of a review committee to submit all proposals for review. It was resolved to organize a review committee divided into administrative and technical groups. The chairman designated Tan Zhongkui, Leng Yuqiu, Ge Yuncheng, Zhu Jingan, Xue Shouxuan, Qian Fenghao, Qi Lunjie, Hou Zhenping, Jiang Nanchun, and Xu Zhen as members of the administrative group review committee, and He Yiqu, Shao Shenpei, Xia Juemin, Sun Benzhong, Fei Kuisheng, Gu Qinghong, Shan Shufu, Yi Tingjian, Tang Xixiang, and Tai Qirui as members of the technical group review committee. A total of twenty-two proposals were submitted. The following were submitted to the administrative group: (1) Implement a silkworm seed control policy in counties in Jiangsu with developed sericulture and provide universal guidance to benefit farmers and reverse the decline of the sericulture industry. (2) Establish central sericulture promotion areas and train sericulture promotion personnel in various parts of Jiangsu Province. (3) Reward high-quality silkworm seeds. (4) County agricultural improvement fields should be attached to rural sericulture training schools. (5) Establish a Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture Prohibition Office. (6) Strictly prohibit silkworm seeds and expand the authority of county fields. (7) Actively develop sericulture in the old Jinling saliva area to reduce silk production costs. (8) Determine that reducing the cost of China silk and giving full play to its inherent quality are the two major administrative guidelines for the Jiangsu silk industry in the future, and submit them to the Ministry of Industry for adoption and implementation so that the whole country can uniformly promote them to save the silk industry from danger. (5) The Wuxi Silk Factory Industry Association submitted a report stating that cocoon merchants collected too many double-stove unsatisfied four-carriage cocoons, which could not be baked in time, and listed reasons for requesting amendments to the regulations to restrict them. (10) Request the Ministry of Industry to consult the Ministry of Transportation and Railways to stipulate silkworm seed transportation methods, and request the Ministry of Finance to appropriately reduce the export tax of various customs for domestic silkworm seed transportation. (10)(1) Formulate a Jiangsu Provincial Silkworm Seed Control Fund. (10)(2) Request that it be determined that silkworm seed control will be implemented throughout the province from the spring of the 22nd year, and that various silkworm seed control regulations be drafted and prepared for implementation as soon as possible. (10)(3) Establish a model silk factory. (10)(4) Fourteen cases such as the Yanzhou Yuhang type were submitted to the technical group: (1) Request to promote textiles to broaden the sales of silk. (2) Silkworm disease prevention and elimination. (3) Establish large-scale provincial mulberry nurseries. (4) Standardize variety names. (5) Improve the Jiangsu mulberry garden. (6) Unify the quality of original silkworm seeds and seek to improve them. (7) Improve sericulture technology. (8) Elect the Central University to actively cultivate senior sericulture talents, study advanced sericulture, improve Chinese mulberry silkworms, and save the Chinese sericulture industry. In addition, the Industrial Department proposed a preliminary plan to improve the sericulture industry in Jiangsu Province, which was submitted to the administrative and technical groups for joint review.

Summary of Draft Resolutions: A total of twenty-three resolutions were made this time. The key points are recorded below. A. Administrative Group (1) The preliminary plan for improving the sericulture industry in Jiangsu was approved in principle and will be handled separately by the Industrial Department. (2) The Industrial Department will organize a sericulture control committee as soon as possible to implement the silkworm seed control policy. (3) Before implementation, the Industrial Department will select appropriate counties to imitate the Jintan County seed sales method to promote improved seeds as much as possible. (4) Promote textiles to broaden the sales of silk. (5) Reward high-quality silkworm seeds. (6) The Industrial Department will designate the Wuxi, Yangzhou, Huaiyin, and Xuzhou provincial fields as central sericulture promotion areas, taking into account the financial situation, and appoint the sericulture personnel in charge of each field as the director of the area to guide the promotion work of the fields near each county. (7) Actively promote sericulture in the old Jinling road area to reduce silk production costs. (8) Prohibit old cocoon shops and promote new-style Hong cocoon machine cocoon shops, and formulate separate cocoon shop reorganization rules to be drafted by the Sericulture Control Committee. (9) Establish a model silk factory. B. Technical Group (1) White spot disease prevention and elimination method. A. Disinfectants should be mainly sulfur and calcium hypochlorite, which are more effective. B. Diseased and dead silkworms should be thrown into lime water or burned, or disinfectant should be sprayed on them. C. Silkworm physical disinfection should be strictly treated with formalin calcium hypochlorite. D. Ectoparasitic insects, which act as a medium for white spot disease transmission, should be removed or exterminated. E. The buying and selling or storage of stiff silkworms in domestic medicinal materials should have a device to prevent the spread of white spot disease spores, otherwise they will be prohibited. (2) Strictly prohibit silkworm seeds, improve sericulture technology, and expand the authority of county fields. (3) Determine that reducing the cost of China silk and giving full play to its inherent quality are the two major administrative guidelines for the Jiangsu silk industry in the future, and submit them to the Ministry of Industry for adoption and implementation so that the entire country can uniformly promote them to save the silk industry from danger. Temporary motion (1) The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Industry will consult with the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction and submit a report to the Ministry of Industry to announce this year's autumn cocoon price. (2) Improve silk fabrics to increase silk sales. (3) Request the provincial government to imitate the Jintan method to add sericulture improvement model areas in appropriate counties and find ways to subsidize them. (4) Request the central government to allocate half of the tax revenue from rayon each year to improve the sericulture production in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. (5) Promote small-scale silk production cooperatives in rural areas. (15th)

◎ The Yellow River is Tense in Both the Upper and Lower Reaches of Shandong Province 86

Continuous Autumn Rain Makes Rescue Difficult

Jinan Correspondence: Continuous overcast and rainy weather has caused the Yellow River's water level to rise again. Moreover, the autumn flood tide is rapid and has strong scouring force, making both the upper and lower reaches tense simultaneously. In the upper reaches, the large slippage at Liuzhuang, on the border between Hebei and Shandong, directly impacts the official office. Hemp sacks are being thrown to protect it. The water level at Lisheng Village has risen by 1.7 cm, and at Qishilibu by 3.4 cm. At Lisheng Village, due to the rapid rise of the water, the heavy slippage is pouring into the fourth, sixth, ninth, and tenth embankments, and the work on each embankment section is heavy. The fifth embankment has already collapsed with the water level, and the head of the sixth embankment has entered the water. A wooden pile in front of the embankment has been broken. The slight slippage at the seventh embankment of Zhukou is being protected. In the lower reaches, the embankments at Huimin and Wangzaojia are collapsing, damaging the embankment base and causing the loss of embankments. Zhang Lianjia, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, together with Gao Daofu, the magistrate of Huimin County, supervised and led the civilians and soldiers to desperately throw hemp sacks and stones to protect the embankment foundation. Today, another 5,000 hemp sacks and 400 ropes were transported from Jinan to Wangzaojia for use. Zhang Lianjia telegraphed the provincial government today to report that it can be guaranteed that there is no danger. At Damajia in the lower reaches, the water has risen by 3.6 cm. The newly built embankments are all stable. The water level at Luokou rose by 2.2 cm this morning and another 8 mm in the afternoon, reaching 29.77 meters. (August 14th)

Local Correspondence

Taicang 87

Refugees Rob More Than Ten Families: In the morning of the day before yesterday, seven large boats from Jiangbei arrived at the town of Huchuanqiao in the county, carrying about two hundred men and women who looked like refugees. The patrol chief of the town's police station, upon hearing the news, immediately ordered the police to escort them out of the territory to avoid disturbance. Unexpectedly, the police returned midway, and the men and women went to Dawan Township on their own. At about 10 o'clock, they landed at Dawan Township and robbed more than ten families, including the head of Dawan Township, Zhu Bosheng, and fled fully loaded, with losses of about a thousand taels of silver. Afterwards, Township Head Zhu reported the incident to the Shuangfeng District Office, which in turn reported it to the County Government and requested an arrest.

Wuxi 88

Drinking Tea Leads to Murder: Sun Quanlian, a native of Ningbo, Zhejiang, opened the Wan Changxiang Foreign Iron Shop on Dongxin Road outside Guangfu Gate. He had four sons. At 8 a.m. on the morning of the 15th, Bai A'gen, aka Bai Xiaoyan, who opened the Bai Rongxing White Iron Shop in Zhoushanbang, Guangqin District, was formerly an apprentice at Wan Changxiang. Recently, he had a dispute with Sun in the same industry due to jealousy. He invited Sun Quanlian and Sun's second son, Dongsheng, to the Dongsheng Tea House to discuss the matter. Unexpectedly, after a disagreement, Bai A'gen punched Sun Dongsheng in the waist, hitting a vital point and killing him on the spot. Quanlian, seeing this, immediately reported it to the police station of the Second Public Security Bureau, who arrested the murderer Bai A'gen and took him to the bureau for interrogation before transferring him to the general bureau for trial. Tian San Tu Tu Zheng Xi Laoliang reported to the County Court and requested an autopsy. At 2 p.m., Prosecutor Shen, accompanied by Wang, the coroner, went to perform the autopsy. The autopsy revealed that the deceased Sun Dongsheng had indeed died from injuries. After the autopsy, he ordered the family of the deceased to prepare a coffin for burial and wait for the Public Security Bureau to send the murderer to the court for further investigation.

Huayu Ferry Destroyed Midway: The China Hengyu Steamboat Company, under the Gongyun Bridge outside the North Gate, has a branch office to facilitate passengers getting on and off the ship. At about 2 p.m. on the 9th of this month, the Huayu Ferry of the Xicao class of the branch office, as usual, sailed from Wuxi to Cao. When passing the Wuqiao branch office, the branch office did not have any passenger tickets sold, so it was assumed that there were no passengers on board and it continued to sail. Unexpectedly, at that time, there were three female students, Wang Xiuying and Qian Huizhen, waiting on the shore to take the ferry to Xinlu Bridge. When they saw the ferry sailing past, they shouted to stop the boat and questioned the branch office. The branch office said that since Wang and others had not purchased tickets, how did they know that they needed to take the ferry? Therefore, there was a disagreement in the language. However, in order to comply with the customer, the ferry was still ordered to stop. However, Wang and others refused to board the boat in anger and walked away. The next day, when the ferry passed Xinlu Bridge, many villagers suddenly blocked the ferry from sailing and questioned the reason for not taking the three women. The captain of the ferry, Xu A'mei, explained in a gentle manner. As a result, the villagers proposed the condition that the Wuqiao branch office should be closed down and a verbal apology should be made for the loss. The ferry then made a false promise to pass. Afterwards, the ferry came to the city and reported the situation to the company. Qian Weiqing, the manager of the company, telegraphed Qian Chongqing in the village to explain the matter. In order to avoid conflicts in the village, the ferry was ordered to temporarily detour to Dongfeng Bridge behind Xinlu Bridge. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 13th, when the ferry was passing Dongfeng Bridge, many villagers blocked and provoked trouble again, and crossed wooden rafts in the bridge hole. Jiang Hanqing, the cook of the ferry, seeing this, used a bamboo pole to push away the wooden raft. Unexpectedly, the villagers, including You Zibing, waded into the water and boarded the boat, smashing all the glass windows. The remaining villagers threw yellow stones at the boat, causing passengers Gu Fugen and cook Jiang Hanqing to be injured. Later, one of the perpetrators, You Zibing, was captured and sent to the Second Public Security Bureau along with the injured. After a preliminary trial by Bureau Member Liu, yesterday (14th), he prepared a document and sent it to the County Public Security Bureau to wait for the transfer to the court for trial.

Smuggling of Opium by Local Merchants Discovered: The Fifth Public Security Bureau outside the North Gate, Jiangyin Lane, discovered Xu Yongsheng carrying opium in front of the Shihe Silk Shop on Bei Dajie on the afternoon of the day before yesterday, and seized fourteen taels of opium and one tael of opium paste. He was taken to the bureau for interrogation. It is reported that the opium was sold in the Zhao Tea Shop under the bridge. In addition to operating a tea business, Zhao often travels back and forth between Shanghai and Wuxi to secretly transport opium, which sells well in urban and rural areas and earns a lot of profits. Xu Yongsheng, originally named Wang Rensen, who was detained the day before yesterday, is from Hutang in Xicheng. At that time, he was carrying opium and passing by the Shihe Silk Shop when he was discovered by Ge A'lan, who smokes red pills. Because he failed to take the opium, he reported the incident to the police. After a preliminary trial by Bureau Chief Peng, he was transferred to the County Public Security Bureau for trial yesterday. It is also reported that Zhao has established three opium trafficking agencies in Wuxi, one in a tea shop under the bridge, one in a Shikumen near the Old Jufeng Garden, and one in his home in Changan Bridge, which have been operating until now without being detected. It is hoped that the public security authorities will pay attention to it and clear the opium.

Changzhou 89

Murder of a Rickshaw Puller: The Murderer Apprehended: There used to be a dispute between rickshaw pullers near Yingchun Bridge in Wuyi, which led to a death. It was later found out that the deceased was Han Maosong and the murderer was Jin Ruisheng. Jin fled without a trace after the accident. Han Maolin, the brother of Han Maosong, happened to meet Jin Ruisheng on the 13th of this month and called the police to arrest him and send him to the Public Security Station outside Xiaobeimen for preliminary interrogation. Ling Ming (Zi Xiaoshan), appointed by the Provincial Finance Department, took office on the evening of the 14th and arrived at the bureau on the 15th to take over.

They arrested Lu Tingbiao and killed the offender Lu Juncai. The body was dragged away. Lu Tingbiao was sent to the county for trial.

Large Quantities of Japanese Coal Transported to Chengbei Outer Huangtian Port: Huachang Company has built a wharf. It was established by a joint stock combination in the year before last, with Yin Zhongren (currently a standing committee member of the Chamber of Commerce) as the manager. The company has always specialized in selling Japanese coal. On the 10th, a Jieli coal ship arrived, loaded with 700 tons of coal. The ship owner and crew were all Japanese. Yesterday (the 13th), the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Corps found out that within ten days, a large amount of Japanese coal had arrived in Yin, protected by armed Japanese. They sent a letter to Yin Zhongren ordering him to send the coal to the County Chamber of Commerce and the County Party Headquarters immediately to prove the truth.

Jiangning Designated as an Autonomous Experimental County: Jiangning County is located in the capital city. The county's political facilities should be a model for the whole country. At the time of active implementation of autonomy, in order to seek the most ideal county autonomy, it is most appropriate to use Jiangning as an experiment. A certain important person in the central government suggested to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and advocated the establishment of the Jiangning Experimental County Design Committee to plan everything. Chairman Gu also believed that it was necessary to establish a model first in preparing for the autonomy of various counties and expressed great sympathy for this suggestion. The letters of appointment have been issued, and the commissioners will soon meet in Beijing to discuss the methods to be implemented.

Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Corps Warns Yilongxiang: Yilongxiang, a Jingguang grocery store in this port, received a letter from the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Corps saying that recently, stores in Zhenjiang have opened and sold sealed enemy goods. Such willingness to be a subjugated country is deeply regrettable. The Corps has achieved results in its work in Shanghai. Now, the general group has sent people to investigate and found that the company has been sparing no effort in selling enemy goods. It is hereby warned to quickly seal up unsold enemy goods and make a quick statement, otherwise the Corps will use the most severe means to deal with it. It is hoped that you will be aware of the danger. A hand grenade and a follow-up letter are attached, etc. The company was surprised to read this letter and has reported the situation to the industry association and asked it to forward it to the Provincial Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to send someone to check whether there is any violation of the regulations on banning enemy goods. It is willing to accept severe punishment.

Shen Bao Education News

Special Issue No. 1 of the National Sports Conference 96

Opening of the National Sports Conference 97

Unprecedented Conference Opens in Beijing at 8 a.m. Today

Sports Experts Discuss Implementation Plan for National Sports

At this time when the country is facing difficulties, the Ministry of Education convened an unprecedented National Sports Conference, the significance of which is far-reaching. The conference will hold its opening ceremony at the Lizhi Society in Beijing at 8 a.m. today and will last for five days until the 20th. The Preparatory Committee has invited three experts, Yuan Dunli, Wu Yunrui, and Hao Gengsheng, to draft the "Implementation Plan for National Sports" and has received more than 200 proposals from all parties. At this conference, the drafted plan will be the main body, and various proposals will be revised into a unified "Implementation Plan for National Sports". This newspaper will publish a special issue during the conference period, publishing conference news as much as possible, and wishing the conference success.

Conference Preparation Process 98

Peng Baichuan, Guo Lianfeng

(I) Origin

In the sixteenth year, when the University Council was first established, it recognized the importance of national physical education.

Unfortunately, organizational changes soon occurred, preventing any achievements from being made. In July of the eighteenth year, the West Lake Exposition in Hangzhou initiated the National Games. The Ministry of Education intended to use the opportunity to convene a National Physical Education Conference in Hangzhou. The association was requested to prepare for it on behalf of the ministry and Mr. Chu Minyi was hired as the head of preparation and Mr. Yuan Dunli and Mr. Huang Zhenhua were hired as the preparatory committee members. Originally, it was scheduled to be held in Hangzhou in September before and after the National Games. Later, because the National Games were postponed to April of the nineteenth year, the Ministry of Education happened to convene the Second National Education Conference around the same time. The work was heavy and it was feared that it would be difficult to handle both. Therefore, it was decided to postpone the conference. At this time, Mr. Chu Minyi went to Belgium to participate in the competition, so the convening of the conference was suspended.

In April of the eighteenth year, the National Government promulgated the National Physical Education Law. Several years have passed and it has not yet been implemented. Although the Ministry of Education and the Training Supervisory Department have consulted several times on the research and discussion of implementation methods, the problems were too many and it was deemed inappropriate to make a hasty decision without careful discussion by experts. In recent years, national public physical education and school physical education have been declining, and the world's physical education trends are also changing rapidly. If we cannot understand the trends and consider the needs of the people, we must quickly formulate and implement physical education guidelines and standards to serve as a guideline for the implementation of physical education in the country. Otherwise, promoting physical education will be nothing more than empty slogans and, at best, will only repeat the mistakes of others.

When national disaster occurred, the dispirited spirit of the people became even more apparent. Comrades, in view of the crisis of the country, believed that promoting national physical education was necessary to revitalize the national spirit and jointly save the country. Director Chu specially reiterated the previous proposal and sent a letter to the Ministry of Education requesting the convening of a conference. Thereupon, the ministry drafted the standards and number of members, together with the budget estimate, and submitted it to the thirty-fourth Executive Yuan meeting, which resolved to pass it and convene the conference in mid-August of this year. The purpose of this conference is not only to discuss practical physical education issues, formulate implementation plans, and standardize training guidelines, but also to cultivate a healthy national physique and cultivate the national spirit of wisdom, benevolence, and courage. Its mission is even more significant.

(II) Organization of the Preparatory Committee

After the Executive Yuan approved the convening of the National Physical Education Conference in August, the first task of the Ministry of Education was to select and appoint preparatory committee members. In order to concentrate various talents, it appointed major figures from all parties, hoping to explore an implementation plan that suits national conditions and adapts to trends. Therefore, Mr. Chu Minyi served as the chairman, and Mr. Zhang Zhijiang, Zhou Yawei, Wu Yunrui, and Huang Mingdao served as members. The relevant主管 personnel of the Ministry of Education, Section Chief Guo Xin Song, Section Chief Gu Shusen, Section Chief Li Zheng, and Baichuan, were also added as members. Later, because Section Chief Guo requested leave and Section Chief Li took the post of Principal of Beijing Normal University and could not return to Beijing temporarily, Counselor Chen Shizhen and Section Chief Zhong Lingxiu were added as members. It was announced on June 16th. Regarding the organization of the preparatory committee, it was originally divided into four sections. Later, because the power was not easy to unify, the system of general manager was adopted. Under the general manager, there were two sections for documents and reception, with several staff members, so that they could easily communicate with each other. The staff of this committee were appointed by the Ministry of Education, with Lianfeng as the general manager and Mr. Yi Kejun as the editor-in-chief of the conference daily. Mr. Gu Liangjie, Huang Longxian, Weng Zhida, Huang Wenqi, Wang Linggen, He Bolie, Gao Hongtu, Jin Guisun, and Wang Zhan served as staff members of the document section. Shi Wei, Zhang Yuanxun, Tu Gang, Shu Chushi, Zai Zefan, Wei Xuezhi, Jia Guoen, Zhu Shusen, and Zou Fengji served as staff members of the reception section. They started working in June.

(III) Important Resolutions of the Preparatory Committee

The Preparatory Committee has held eight meetings up to August 12. The important resolutions are listed below:

(First Committee Meeting) Held on June 16, the main resolutions were: 1. Passed the organizational outline of the National Physical Education Conference Preparatory Committee. 2. Passed the rules of procedure of the National Physical Education Conference. 3. Requested the Ministry of Education to separately send letters to inform various agencies and national and registered colleges and universities to send representatives to attend the conference and submit proposals before August 1.

(Second Committee Meeting) Held on June 17, the main resolutions were: 1. Hired Mr. Yuan Dunli, Wu Yunrui, and Hao Gengsheng as members of the National Physical Education Implementation Plan Drafting Committee to develop a complete plan. 2. Passed the rules of procedure of the National Physical Education Conference. 3. Passed the rules of examination of proposals of the National Physical Education Conference. 4. Passed the rules of audience of the National Physical Education Conference. 5. Decided that the meeting place and the accommodation for members would be at the Lihgishe Society.

(Third Committee Meeting) Held on July 1, the main resolutions were: 1. Decided that August 16 to 21 would be the date for receiving members. 2. Selected and hired Zhang Boling, Du Tingxiu, Zhang Xinfu, Ma Yuehan, Fang Wanbang, Dong Shouyi, Ma Liang, Wu Jianquan, Xu Zhiyi, Chen Lingyun, Liu Shenyan, and Xu Yanzhi as experts. 3. Decided that the preparatory committee members and the plan drafting committee members would be ex officio members. 4. Those who are related to the physical education field but cannot be hired as experts will be specially invited by the preparatory committee or the Ministry of Education to attend the conference. 5. Passed the reception rules. 6. Decided to manufacture badges and manuals, etc. 7. Decided on the date of the meeting.

(Fourth Committee Meeting) Held on July 15, the main resolutions were: 1. Hired Chen Jiaji, Gu Guruo, and Zhang Yuanyang as experts. 2. Granted the Shantou branch of the Guangdong Provincial Physical Education Association permission to send representatives to attend the conference.

(Fifth Committee Meeting) Held on July 26, the main resolutions were: 1. Requested that the Standard Sports Equipment Company send domestically produced sports equipment to the conference for display and requested that the Ministry of Education consult the Ministry of Railways to order the Jinghu Railway to handle it free of charge.

(Sixth Committee Meeting) Held on August 2, the main resolutions were: 1. Granted the Shanghai Chinese Physical Education Association permission to send representatives to attend the conference. 2. Granted the Shanghai Jingwu Physical Education Association permission to send representatives to attend the conference. 3. Proposals sent by various members and agencies will be mimeographed immediately and a temporary proposal sorting committee will be organized, with the preparatory committee members serving as members and inviting several experts to assist. Committee member Wu Yunrui will be responsible for convening all of this.

(I) Chairman of the Congress, Zhu Jiahua. (II) Chairman of the Congress and Director of the Preparatory Committee, Chu Minyi. (III) Zhang Zhijiang, Preparatory Committee Member of the Congress.

(IV) Work of This Committee

I. Staff Meeting: After the Ministry of Education appointed the staff of the Preparatory Committee by ministry order, the first staff meeting was held on June 21 to assign work. The important resolutions are as follows: (1) Staff Dai Zefan is responsible for drawing the design of the committee's badge, and Staff Weng Zhida, Huang Longxian, and Gu Liangjie are responsible for drafting the manual. Staff Shi Wei is responsible for contacting the printing company. (3) Staff Tu Gang of the committee's budget is responsible for reviewing it and requesting the Ministry of Education to submit it to the Accounting Office. (4) Assigned the duties of the document section staff, including four people for meeting records, three people for editing the conference daily, two people for sorting proposals and preparing the agenda, and the general manager will assign people to draft, receive, and send documents at any time. (5) Assigned the duties of the reception section staff. Staff Shi Wei will be in charge of administrative matters, Staff Tu Gang will be in charge of accounting matters, and Staff Zhang Yuanxun will be in charge of all conference matters at the venue and dormitory. Three people will be in charge of dormitory reception, and four people will be in charge of venue reception, divided into two groups. Two people in each group will be in charge of registration and receiving audience tickets, and two people will be in charge of venue reception and distributing proposals and printed materials. (6) Contacted the Central Hospital to arrange for the health of the members.

(II) Contacted the Lihgishe Society for the venue and dormitory. The venue selection was quite painstaking. The distance between the members' accommodation and the venue was too far, which was not only inconvenient for traveling back and forth and wasted transportation costs, but also made it difficult for the staff to take measures. The difficulties felt during the first and second education conferences must be avoided. Therefore, it was decided to contact the Lihgishe Society to negotiate the lease of the auditorium and dormitory dining halls, etc. All of these have been negotiated, and Director General Huang of the society has agreed to make all the facilities available to the members as much as possible. (III) Handled the reduction of ticket prices for members' rides. After several contacts with the Ministry of Railways, all kinds of difficulties have been eliminated. The Ministry of Education has distributed the discount certificates to each member for their use.

(IV) Made badges. The style of the badges worn by members and staff has been handed over to the Standard Sports Equipment Company to manufacture 200 silver embossed badges and 220 silk ribbons. The company has sent representatives to deliver them. The style is very beautiful and can be distributed and worn during the meeting.

(V) Sorting and printing of proposals. As of August 13, more than 210 proposals have been received. However, the text format of the proposals is very inconsistent. Therefore, the committee will first make a preliminary sorting and classification. As for merging and revising, it should be handled by the review committee of the conference. The staff of the committee are stepping up their work to print the proposals separately so that they can be distributed to each member during the meeting.

(VI) Members are enthusiastic. The names of more than 110 members have been reported to the committee. Nanjing, Qinghai, Jiangsu, Chahar, Yunnan, Gansu, Jiangxi, Qingdao, Anhui, Shanghai, Guizhou, Henan, Shandong, Shaanxi, Hebei, Fujian, Zhejiang, Hubei, Suiyuan, Guangxi, Hunan, Guangdong, and Hong Kong have all sent representatives to attend the conference. The remaining provinces, such as Shanxi, Ningxia, and Rehe, have sent letters stating that they cannot send representatives.

(VII) The Standard Sports Equipment Company and Liangyou Sports Goods Manufacturing Co., Ltd. will send domestically produced sports equipment to the conference for display and have agreed on the display methods. The committee will sincerely welcome any domestically produced sports equipment that is sent to the conference for display.

(VIII) During the conference, in order to allow members to understand the national physical education situation, survey forms have been printed and distributed to national and registered colleges and universities and education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities to fill in the physical education overview forms for reference during the meeting.

(IX) In past conferences held by the government, members have suffered from too much feasting. Most of the members of this conference are physical education experts. Therefore, the method of entertainment for members is mainly sports, and it is planned to ask the Film Censorship Committee to collect films on sports and national disasters for screening at the conference.

(X) The committee plans to use the various facilities of the Central Sports Field to allow the members of the committee to practice and perform as much as possible.

(XI) In order to arouse the members' interest in national martial arts, the committee has negotiated with the Central National Martial Arts Hall to schedule performances.

(XII) In order to allow celebrities of the Party and the country to express their opinions on national physical education, the Ministry of Education has separately sent letters to various celebrities to come to the conference to give speeches on a regular basis.

The above is just a summary of the major points. I hope you can give us your guidance.

Yesterday's Preparatory Meeting 99

Taking the National Physical Education Implementation Plan as the Blueprint. Nanjing, 15th telegram. The ninth preparatory meeting of the National Physical Education Conference at 2 p.m. on the 15th. Yuan, Wu, and Hao, the committee members in charge of drafting the plan, also attended the meeting. Chairman Chu Minyi resolved the following: (1) Preparatory committee member Huang Mingdao entrusted Jiang Xiangqing to represent him due to illness. The resolution was approved to allow him to attend the meeting. (2) The Hong Kong Sports Association sent Zhao Qianghua to attend the meeting. (3) The board of directors of the Zhongshan Sports College has been registered. Can they attend the meeting? (4) The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has certified that the Southeast Women's Physical Education Normal School has been registered. Should they be allowed to attend the meeting? (5) It is confirmed that Cheng Lie Sports School has requested registration, but six points have been pointed out to be revised, which has delayed the official business. Should they be allowed to attend the meeting? The above four cases were all resolved to allow them to attend the meeting. (6) It was resolved to amend the examination rules, canceling the original seven groups and changing them to five groups (Goals) (Administrative Organization) (Research) (Implementation and Promotion) (Evaluation and Others), each group including national martial arts. (7) If the plan drafting committee members and experts are sent as representatives, should their expert qualifications be canceled according to Article 3 of the regulations, and what kind of treatment should they receive? The case was resolved to attend the meeting with the qualifications of representatives, and the travel expenses will be paid by the representative organization. The meeting will send a letter to inform them. (8) It was resolved that each newspaper reporter or news agency will only be given one copy of the proposal per museum. (9) Restricted temporary motions. The resolution was passed by the chairman to the examination committee. (10) The first meeting agenda was resolved. (11) It was resolved to revise and enrich the implementation plan, taking the National Physical Education Implementation Plan as the blueprint, and then revising it with the proposals and resolutions to form a complete National Physical Education Implementation Plan. (12) The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission requested that two representatives from Mongolia and Tibet attend the meeting. The resolution was passed that one representative from Mongolia and Tibet would be allowed to attend the meeting.

The Drafting Process of the National Physical Education Plan 100

Wu Yunrui

Recently, the government has been seeking the unification of national politics and education and has held national military conferences, national financial conferences, and national education conferences, etc. The intentions are very good. However, due to the repeated internal and external troubles and the instability of the political situation and economy, the resolutions are rarely implemented, which is a pity. This time, Mr. Chu Minyi initiated the National Physical Education Conference to seek the unification of physical education and increase the effectiveness of promotion. At this time of national crisis, it is indeed an important plan to seek self-rescue. If it can avoid repeating the mistakes of other conferences, the government will gradually implement important resolutions.

And the foundation of a strong country will also be firmly established from now on. Although the responsibility for the implementation of the proposal lies with the government, the conference itself should be responsible for the relevance and systematicness of the proposal for easy implementation. After Mr. Yuan Dunli and Hao Gengsheng were entrusted with the task of drafting the plan, after several days of consideration, they all advocated that the drafting of the plan should be organized and systematic to avoid the disadvantages of being scattered and fragmented. After the outline was drafted, the comrades in Peiping were asked to criticize and revise it before drafting it. After the draft was completed, the comrades were asked to revise it again. However, I was still afraid that the content was not broad enough and the views were too narrow. Therefore, more than 100 copies of the draft were printed and distributed to physical education leaders in various cities for their comments. On the 22nd of last month, countless opinions were collected. Therefore, the plan was slightly expanded to accommodate as much as possible. Therefore, although there were only three drafters of this plan, dozens of people participated in the opinions. This is because it concerns the whole country and cannot be taken lightly. Proposals are like fish, shrimp, snails, and clams in the water, and the plan is like a net in the river that accommodates everything. When sorting out the proposals, the author first extracts the outline of the plan as various category names, and then classifies them according to the nature of the proposals. If the proposals have no destination, the author inserts other items in the plan according to their nature and lists them. At the meeting, the plan will be discussed in the order of the plan, along with the related proposals. When the discussion of the plan is over, the proposals will also come to an end. Therefore, the result of this conference is to obtain a concrete and systematic plan, and all the proposals are only materials for revising and expanding this plan. The important issues to be resolved in this conference are approximately several:

(I) Administrative Organization: If there are no physical education administrative personnel in the physical education administrative agencies at all levels to promote and inspect, the curriculum standards, etc. specified in all plans will never be realized.

(II) Harmony between Physical Education and National Martial Arts: In the past, those who studied physical education did not talk about national martial arts, and those who practiced national martial arts rejected physical education. Both sides were wrong. In fact, national martial arts cannot be divided from physical education, and physical education cannot be abandoned. It is hoped that this conference can have a reasonable solution.

(III) Tai Chi Ball Exercise: Tai Chi Ball is a newly invented exercise whose function is similar to the medicine ball in Germany, which is several times better than the previous Swedish gymnastics. It should also have a considerable position in physical education. However, national martial artists discriminate against it. It is also necessary to discuss it calmly and reach a satisfactory conclusion in this conference.

General Overview of the Venue Layout 104

The Magnificent and Splendid National Spirit Fellowship Society

Comprehensive Arrangement of the Grand Auditorium

The Preparatory Committee of the National Athletic Meet, in order to cater to the members' meals and lodging, dispatched personnel to negotiate with Mr. Huang Renlin, the executive secretary of the Society. It was agreed to borrow the grand auditorium as the venue for the congress and use all the dormitories for the members' accommodation. This arrangement places the venue and accommodation in the same location, saving travel time and indirectly increasing the efficiency of the meeting. The Society is located east of Huangpu Road, facing Zhongshan Road, making transportation very convenient. Its three palatial new buildings, with vermilion bricks and green rafters, are magnificent and splendid, and are famous new structures in the capital. The auditorium is located in the northwest. Its construction was proposed by the Women's Comforting Soldiers Association, which donated eighty thousand yuan from surplus funds raised for comforting the troops to the Society for the purpose of building the auditorium to commemorate the meritorious deeds of the soldiers who quelled the rebellions. The intention is excellent. The exterior of the auditorium resembles a palace, while the interior is a stage-style lecture hall. The lower level serves as the venue for sports conferences, the upper level consists of superior box seats, and the top level is the projection room. It is said that meetings will be held during the day, and various sports films will be screened in the evening to meet the members' needs for observation and entertainment, truly achieving two purposes with one action. The exterior of the auditorium is surrounded by flowers and a road lined with green cypresses. The short grass is like a carpet, and the capital's famous tennis court is located there, surrounded by lead netting and equipped with perfect facilities. Sports members can try their hand at tennis during breaks from the meeting to relax. As for the interior of the venue, due to the Society's cadre training class currently holding its graduation ceremony, arrangements cannot be completed until the afternoon of the 15th.

Proposals are Divided into Five Categories 108

231 Proposals Received

The congress hired Yuan Dunli (Chairman), Wu Yunrui, and Hao Gengsheng to draft the "National Physical Education Plan." 231 proposals were received from various parties and classified as follows:

(1) "Goals": Physical education goals

(2) "Administrative Organization": Physical education administration, physical education funding, physical education equipment, various physical education gatherings and organizations, physical education achievement exhibitions, five-year plan.

(3) "Research": Curriculum, teaching materials, physical education research, physical education books.

(4) "Implementation and Promotion": Teacher training, teacher development, studying abroad, teacher qualifications, teacher treatment, military training, mass physical education, children's physical education, military physical education.

(5) "Evaluation and Others"

Five Provisional Proposals 109

Nanjing, 15th - The deadline for congress proposals is the 15th. There are many provisional proposals from members, which, according to regulations, must be co-signed by ten people to be submitted. It is now known that Chen Baiqing, a representative from Zhejiang, proposed that all levels of government agencies should implement physical examinations for future employees to set an example for the people. The Zhejiang National Arts Institute submitted four proposals co-signed by Zhang Zhijiang: (1) All divisions, brigades, regiments, and battalions of the military should add National Arts training; (2) The Ministry of Education should stipulate that physical education teachers should be proficient in National Arts; (3) Establish a National Arts Normal School; (4) The Ministry of Education should issue a circular to all levels of schools to include National Arts as a required subject.

Various Aspects of the Conference 111

Huang Mingdao Sends a Representative to Attend

Jiang Xiangqing Also Serves as a Representative of the National Physical Education Association

Huang Mingdao, director of the Chinese National Physical Education Association and manager of the Ta Da Bank, enthusiastically promotes physical education and spares no effort. He has held important positions in past Far Eastern and National Games, especially during the 8th Far Eastern Games held in Shanghai, when the revolutionary army was rising and there were no funds available for the meeting. At that time, Huang was the chairman of the Economic Committee of the congress, and he relied on his efforts alone to raise tens of thousands of yuan from various parties to enable the congress to be successfully completed. As the Ministry of Education is holding a National Physical Education Conference, Huang has also been hired as a member of the preparatory committee. He originally intended to come to Beijing as soon as possible to support everything, but due to illness for nine months, he could not fulfill his wish. Therefore, he sent a letter to the Ministry of Education appointing Jiang Xiangqing as his representative to attend. In addition, the Chinese National Physical Education Association noted that some of the proposals at this conference were closely related to the Association, so it sent a letter to Chairman Chu Minyi, requesting that Jiang Xiangqing also be a representative to facilitate various consultations when necessary.

Chairman Chu and the committee members proposed that experts should be added to each of the five groups that had already been determined. During the formal meeting, each expert will join the group review meeting separately.

Nanjing, 15th - The conference funds have not yet been received. In order to save expenses, the reception group will close the reception desk at the Central Hotel starting on the 16th, and experts and members will move into the National Spirit Fellowship Society.

Opinions of Graduates of the Physical Education Department of National Southeast University

The alumni association of the Physical Education Department of National Southeast University, National Higher Normal School, and National Central University congratulates this National Physical Education Conference and offers three points of advice: (1) Summarize proposals, simplify complexity, and integrate parts into a systemic whole in administrative terms to create an overall plan. (2) Have high aspirations but start with small steps. Eliminate sectarian bias and gather collective wisdom to find the root cause and solve the current situation based on national conditions and popular sentiments. (3) Ensure that resolutions can be implemented and realized after the conference.

Closing of the 10th World Games 112

(Elect Telegraph 14th, Los Angeles) The 10th World Olympic Games, which began on July 30th, concluded here this afternoon at 2:00 PM with the equestrian jumping event as the final act. The awards ceremony and closing ceremony were held one after another. Spectators from various countries vied to witness this grand ceremony, scrambling to enter the venue early in the morning. The grandstands around the perimeter were full, leaving no room to stand, with a crowd of approximately 120,000 people. At 1:30 PM, the obstacles for the equestrian competition were neatly arranged, with red and white flags marking the positions of the obstacles. At 2:00 PM, a platform was set up in front of the main grandstand for the winners, with officials from various countries lined up in front. At 2:10 PM, the awards ceremony began. The winner of the boxing event was invited to the platform. Amidst applause and cheers from the crowd, the national flag of the winning country was hoisted high, and the national anthem of the winning country was sung.

The awards ceremony was temporarily suspended, and the final equestrian jumping competition was held. Athletes from various countries, led by France, marched in formation. Then, the French athlete, the winner, demonstrated equestrian skills, galloping east and west. At times, the rider seemed detached from the saddle, and at other times, the horse seemed separated from its rider, a spectacle of wondrous skill. The audience marveled and sighed. Next, the jumping competition was held. Japanese Major Imamura fell from his horse at the fifth obstacle after jumping over the fourth. When he remounted and jumped at the eighth obstacle, the horse disobeyed three times and he was eliminated. Athlete Yoshida withdrew due to injury. Athlete Xi won first place.

At 3:30 PM, the awards ceremony resumed. Awards were presented for all track and field events, including the triple jump, pole vault, long jump, and high jump, as well as all water sports. The Olympic medals were also awarded to winners from various countries in succession. At 5:00 PM (9:00 AM on the 15th, Shanghai time), the awards ceremony was completely finished, and the closing ceremony immediately followed. After the music played, Count Henri de Baillet-Latour, the president of the International Olympic Committee, stood on the podium and delivered the closing speech, which generally stated that the 10th Olympic Games had been completed in an orderly and satisfactory manner, and that he expressed his deep gratitude to the Mayor and citizens of Los Angeles and the representatives of various countries. After the speech, five ceremonial cannons were fired, and the resounding military music played. The Olympic flag was taken down and handed by President Baillet-Latour to Los Angeles Mayor Bowron, asking him to keep it until the 11th Games in 1936. The Olympic flame, which had been burning above the main gate of the Games since July 30th, was then extinguished. More than 2,000 athletes from all over the world marched out of the venue in formation. The Games were completely concluded. The National News Agency in Los Angeles reported on the 14th that the 10th World Games, which shook the world, concluded with the awards ceremony today. The number of spectators exceeded that of previous sessions. Newspaper commentaries praised the results as being exceptionally excellent, with many new world and Olympic records created.

Summer Football League: Huadong Football Team vs. Yuqing 113

Today at 5:15 PM at the Baseball Field

The Huadong and Yuqing football teams will play against each other at the baseball field at 5:15 PM today as part of the Summer League. Referee: Chen Jixiang. (Note: The match between Lingnan B and Dajiang has been rescheduled.)
